GEOTECHNICAL ENGINEERING TESTING 
BRADSHAW ARMY AIRFIELD AT POHAKULOA TRAINING AREA 
ISLAND OF HAWAI’I, HAWAI’I 
Dear Mr. Mitchener: 
In accordance with the project specifications and requirements, mooring tests were 
conducted on newly installed mooring eyes for the Bradshaw Army Airfield at Pohakuloa 
Training Area, on the island of Hawai’i, Hawai’i project between May 15 and 25, 2018.  
This letter report summarizes our observation and presents the mooring testing results. 
The mooring tests were conducted on mooring eyes embedded into the airfield 
helicopter pads. Geolabs did not observe the installation of the mooring eyes. The mooring 
tests were conducted in general accordance with ASTM D3689 (Standard Test Methods 
for Deep Foundation Under Static Axial Tensile Load) modified per UFC 3-260-01. 
Based on the approved mooring testing procedures, the testing loads were applied 
on the mooring eyes incrementally in the vertical direction, using a hydraulic jack system. 
The calibration data of the hydraulic jack is included in the Appendix for reference. A steel 
beam was supported on a cribbing system placed at two ends of the beam, providing the 
reaction support. 
Each testing load was measured by a pressure gauge attached on the hydraulic 
jack. The displacement of the testing mooring eyes was measured with a dial gage 
supported on an independent surveyor’s tripod. Typical mooring testing setup is illustrated 
in the photo below. 
Total of 110 mooring eyes were tested. Locations of the testing mooring eyes are 
shown on Plates 1.1 through 1.3. In general, the maximum mooring testing load of about 
5,138 pounds was applied to the mooring eyes in 500-pound load increments. Each load 
increment, including the maximum testing load, was held for at least 1 minute. 
Subsequently, the mooring eyes was unloaded in approximately three decrements. The 
results of the mooring tests are summarized and presented on Plates 2.1 through 2.4. 
Nan Inc. 
Page 2 
W.O. 7709-00 
June 19, 2018 
GEOLABS, INC. 
Hawaii • California 
Detailed information and data collected during the mooring tests are presented on Plates 
3.1 through 3.220. 
Total displacement at the maximum testing load ranged between 0.036 inches to 
0.119 inches. Based on our field observations and the mooring tests conducted, it is our 
professional opinion that the mooring eyes tested for the project are capable of supporting 
the design load capacity without excessive displacement and pull-out failure. 
Nan Inc. Page 3
W.O. 7709-00
June 19, 2018
We appreciate the opportunity to provide our services to you on this project. If you
have questions or need additional information, please contact our office.
Respectfully submitted,

PROFESSIONAL
